	focus = {
		id = PER_descend_on_iraq
		icon = saddamsreign

		x = -1
		y = 1

		relative_position_id = PER_the_road_to_jerusalem

		cost = 5

		prerequisite = { focus = PER_the_road_to_jerusalem }

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_FOREIGN_POLICY FOCUS_FILTER_INFLUENCE }

		available = {
			has_war = no
			IRQ = {
				has_war = no
				has_country_leader = { name = "Saddam Hussein" ruling_only = yes }
				influence_higher_30 = yes
			}
		}

		bypass = { IRQ = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Saddam Hussein" ruling_only = yes } } } }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [THIS.GetName]: Focus PER_descend_on_iraq"
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_coup_against_saddam_TT
			IRQ = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { influence_array^0 = PER } }
					set_temp_variable = { iran_influence_percentage = influence_array_val^0 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { influence_array^1 = PER } }
					set_temp_variable = { iran_influence_percentage = influence_array_val^1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { influence_array^2 = PER } }
					set_temp_variable = { iran_influence_percentage = influence_array_val^2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { influence_array^3 = PER } }
					set_temp_variable = { iran_influence_percentage = influence_array_val^3 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { influence_array^4 = PER } }
					set_temp_variable = { iran_influence_percentage = influence_array_val^4 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { influence_array^5 = PER } }
					set_temp_variable = { iran_influence_percentage = influence_array_val^5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { influence_array^6 = PER } }
					set_temp_variable = { iran_influence_percentage = influence_array_val^6 }
				}
				else = { set_temp_variable = { iran_influence_percentage = 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { iraq_domestic_influence_var = domestic_influence_amount }
				set_temp_variable = { iraq_emerging_outlook_percentage = party_popularity@communism }
				multiply_temp_variable = { iraq_emerging_outlook_percentage = 100 }
				set_temp_variable = { iraq_not_emerging_popularity = 100 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { iraq_not_emerging_popularity = iraq_emerging_outlook_percentage }

				#Chances

				#Coup
				set_temp_variable = { coup_chance = 0 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { coup_chance = iran_influence_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { coup_chance = 30 }

				#Civil War
				set_temp_variable = { civil_war_chance = 0 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { civil_war_chance = 30 } #Makes civil war easier.
				add_to_temp_variable = { civil_war_chance = iraq_emerging_outlook_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { coup_chance = iran_influence_percentage }

				#Nothing happens
				set_temp_variable = { fail_chance = 0 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { fail_chance = iraq_not_emerging_popularity }
				add_to_temp_variable = { fail_chance = iraq_domestic_influence_var }
				add_to_temp_variable = { fail_chance = -50 } #Makes civil war easier.
			}
			random_list = {
				coup_chance = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = PER_iraq_coup
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_opinion_modifier = {
							target = IRQ
							modifier = iraqi_chemical_weapons
						}
						remove_opinion_modifier = {
							target = IRQ
							modifier = oppresses_shiites
						}

						IRQ = {
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = communism
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							set_political_party = {
								ideology = communism
								popularity = 100
							}
							set_temp_variable = { party_index = 9 }
							set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 1.00 }
							add_relative_party_popularity = yes

							set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 9 }
							change_ruling_party_effect = yes

							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = USA
								relation = military_access
								active = no
							}
							USA = {
								diplomatic_relation = {
									country = IRQ
									relation = military_access
									active = no
								}
							}

							swap_ideas = {
								remove_idea = the_military
								add_idea = iranian_quds_force
							}

							swap_ideas = {
								remove_idea = sunni
								add_idea = shia
							}

							create_country_leader = {
								name = "Hadi al-Amiri"
								picture = "Hadi_Al-Amiri.dds"
								ideology = Vilayat_e_Faqih
								traits = {
									emerging_Vilayat_e_Faqih
								}
							}

							remove_opinion_modifier = {
								target = PER
								modifier = oppresses_sunni
							}

							set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 10.00 }
							set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
							set_temp_variable = { influence_target = IRQ }
							change_influence_percentage = yes
						}
					}
				}

 		icon = war_against_israel

		y = 1

			focus = PER_armored_equipment_production
			focus = PER_air_equipment_production
			focus = PER_naval_equipment_production
		}

		cost = 7.15 # 50 Days
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MILITARY }

			is_faction_leader = yes
			num_faction_members > 1
			any_allied_country = {
				has_idea = shia
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_idea = shia is_ally_with = PER NOT = { original_tag = PER } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = PER_aor_ground
							has_idea = PER_aor_air
							has_idea = PER_aor_naval
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_idea = PER_aor_ground }
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = PER_aor_ground
							add_idea = PER_aor_israel_ground
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_idea = PER_aor_air }
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = PER_aor_air
							add_idea = PER_aor_israel_air
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_idea = PER_aor_naval }
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = PER_aor_naval
							add_idea = PER_aor_israel_naval
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_ideas = PER_aor_israel_ground
					}

				}
				else = { add_ideas = PER_aor_israel_ground }
			}
		}
